```diff
 "use client";
 
 import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
 import { useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
 import { SearchInput } from "@/components/ui/search-input";
 import { EntitySidebar } from "@/components/explorer/entity-sidebar";
 import { IssueSidebar } from "@/components/explorer/issue-sidebar";
 import { SearchResults } from "@/components/search/search-results";
 import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
 import { api, LegalUnitSummary, EntityItem } from "@/lib/api";
 import { Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
 
 export default function ExplorerPage() {
     const searchParams = useSearchParams();
     const queryParam = searchParams.get("q") || "";
 
     const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("entities");
     const [selectedEntity, setSelectedEntity] = useState<EntityItem | null>(null);
     const [selectedIssue, setSelectedIssue] = useState<{ year: number; issue_number: number } | null>(null);
     const [results, setResults] = useState<LegalUnitSummary[]>([]);
     const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
 
     // Clear other selection when switching tabs or making a selection
     useEffect(() => {
         if (activeTab === "entities") setSelectedIssue(null);
         if (activeTab === "issues") setSelectedEntity(null);
     }, [activeTab]);
 
     useEffect(() => {
         const performSearch = async () => {
             setLoading(true);
             try {
                 // Determine if we should search
                 const hasSelection = selectedEntity || selectedIssue;
                 const q = queryParam || (hasSelection ? " " : "");
 
                 if (!q) {
                     setResults([]);
                     setLoading(false);
                     return;
                 }
 
                 const res = await api.search(q, 50, {
                     entity_id: selectedEntity?.id,
                     year: selectedIssue?.year,
                     issue_number: selectedIssue?.issue_number
                 });
                 setResults(res.results);
             } catch (e) {
                 console.error(e);
             } finally {
                 setLoading(false);
             }
         };
 
         performSearch();
     }, [queryParam, selectedEntity, selectedIssue]);
 
     return (
         <main className="min-h-screen bg-white dark:bg-slate-950 pt-20 pb-10 px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
             <div className="max-w-[1600px] mx-auto flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-8">
-                {/* Sidebar */}
-                <div className="w-full lg:w-80 flex-shrink-0 h-auto lg:h-[calc(100vh-8rem)] lg:sticky lg:top-24 flex flex-col gap-4">
-                    <Tabs defaultValue="entities" value={activeTab} onValueChange={setActiveTab} className="w-full h-full flex flex-col">
-                        <TabsList className="w-full grid grid-cols-2 mb-4">
-                            <TabsTrigger value="entities">Entities</TabsTrigger>
-                
... (truncated, 7766 chars total)
```

```diff
 "use client";
 
 import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
 import { useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
 import { SearchInput } from "@/components/ui/search-input";
 import { EntitySidebar } from "@/components/explorer/entity-sidebar";
 import { IssueSidebar } from "@/components/explorer/issue-sidebar";
 import { SearchResults } from "@/components/search/search-results";
 import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
 import { api, LegalUnitSummary, EntityItem } from "@/lib/api";
 import { Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
 
+import { Sidebar } from "@/components/layout/Sidebar";
+
 export default function ExplorerPage() {
     const searchParams = useSearchParams();
     const queryParam = searchParams.get("q") || "";
 
     const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("entities");
     const [selectedEntity, setSelectedEntity] = useState<EntityItem | null>(null);
     const [selectedIssue, setSelectedIssue] = useState<{ year: number; issue_number: number } | null>(null);
     const [results, setResults] = useState<LegalUnitSummary[]>([]);
     const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
 
     // Clear other selection when switching tabs or making a selection
     useEffect(() => {
         if (activeTab === "entities") setSelectedIssue(null);
         if (activeTab === "issues") setSelectedEntity(null);
     }, [activeTab]);
 
     useEffect(() => {
         const performSearch = async () => {
             setLoading(true);
             try {
                 // Determine if we should search
                 const hasSelection = selectedEntity || selectedIssue;
                 const q = queryParam || (hasSelection ? " " : "");
 
                 if (!q) {
                     setResults([]);
                     setLoading(false);
                     return;
                 }
 
                 const res = await api.search(q, 50, {
                     entity_id: selectedEntity?.id,
                     year: selectedIssue?.year,
                     issue_number: selectedIssue?.issue_number
                 });
                 setResults(res.results);
             } catch (e) {
                 console.error(e);
             } finally {
                 setLoading(false);
             }
         };
 
         performSearch();
     }, [queryParam, selectedEntity, selectedIssue]);
 
     return (
-        <main className="min-h-screen bg-white dark:bg-slate-950 pt-20 pb-10 px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
-            <div className="max-w-[1600px] mx-auto flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-8">
-                {/* Main Content */}
-                <div className="flex-1 space-y-6">
-                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
-                        <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-slate-900 dark:text-white">Explorer</h1>
-                        <p className="text-slate-500">
-                            {activeTab === "entities"
-                                ? "Filter documents by Peop
```

```diff
 # Walkthrough - Authentication & Bookmarks Implemented
 
 ## Overview
 I have successfully implemented the Authentication and Bookmarking features for La Gazette. Users can now sign up, log in, manage their personal library of legal documents, and organize them into folders.
 
 ## Changes
 
 ### Authentication
 - **Supabase Integration**: Configured Supabase Auth for Email/Password and Google sign-in.
 - **Frontend Pages**: Created `/login` and `/signup` pages with form validation and error handling.
+- **Interactive Term Cards**: Clean, professional cards explaining terms like Decree, Law, Decision, and Circular with context.
+- **Rights Section**: Categorized list of fundamental rights (Civil, Political, Socio-Economic) with constitutional citations.
 - **Global Context**: Implemented `AuthProvider` to manage user sessions across the application.
 
 ### Bookmarks & Library
 - **Database Schema**: Created `bookmarks` and `folders` tables.
 - **Library Page**: Created `/library` where users can:
     - View all bookmarked documents.
     - Create and delete folders.
     - Organize bookmarks (MVP level).
 - **Bookmark Button**: Integrated a toggle button on the Legal Unit Detail page to instantly save/unsave documents.
 
+![Information Page & Sidebar](/Users/louaimroueh/.gemini/antigravity/brain/36d823b9-69c1-471c-b768-5647760014e8/information_page_fixed_1771353187680.png)
+![Explorer Layout](/Users/louaimroueh/.gemini/antigravity/brain/36d823b9-69c1-471c-b768-5647760014e8/explorer_page_fixed_1771353216480.png)
+
 ### Backend Optimizations
 - **Performance Fix**: Drastically reduced query limits in `SearchService` (from 100k to 2k-5k rows) to prevent the development server from hanging during statistics retrieval.
 - **Startup Fix**: Resolved an environment variable issue in `auth.py` ensuring specific Supabase keys are used correctly for backend client initialization.
 
 ## verification
 - **Backend Health**: Verified backend starts up correctly and responds to health checks (`GET /` -> 200 OK).
 - **Frontend Connectivity**: Confirmed frontend serves pages and attempts to connect to backend.
 - **Performance**: API response for health check is now immediate (<100ms), whereas previously it could hang due to heavy data loading.
 
 ## Next Steps
 - **Search & Filter in Library**: Add search functionality specific to the user's library.
 - **Drag & Drop**: Implement drag-and-drop for moving bookmarks into folders.
 - **Advanced Auth**: Add password reset and profile update features.
```
